## 歌词

<div>
In the valley, <br><br>
in the pretty star,<br><br>
I saw the shinning light,<br><br>
out of your smile.<br><br>
Am I hurting you <br><br>
on your broken heart? <br><br>
Am I a mean trick man<br><br>
with twisted mind?<br><br>
It’s a sappy song in a word<br><br>
lacking all the trust, <br><br>
wearing all the skins, <br><br>
sparking in the sun. <br><br>
On shallow underground, <br><br>
people are born to pay. <br><br>
They are trying to find a way <br><br>
to the pale living place.<br><br>
In the valley, <br><br>
in the pretty star, <br><br>
I saw the shinning light <br><br>
out of your smile.<br><br>
It’s a sappy song in a word,<br><br>
lacking all the trust, <br><br>
wearing all the skins, <br><br>
sparking in the sun.<br><br>
Leaking on the ground,<br><br>
sailing on the boat, <br><br>
are you suffering all the pains? <br><br>
Are you tasting all the blames?<br><br>
Wearing all the skins, <br><br>
dropping all the faces,<br><br>
Am I wasting all your time? <br><br>
Am I killing all your life? <br><br>
To the end of all my road, <br><br>
to the sunrise all alone, <br><br>
are you shifting to below? <br><br>
Are you dating me alone? <br><br>
To the end of all my road, <br><br>
to the sunrise all alone, <br><br>
are you shifting to below? <br><br>
Are you dating me alone? <br><br>
Are you shaken from the words? <br><br>
Are you shaking from the world? <br><br>
Are you dating me alone?<br><br>
Are you cheating me lone? <br><br>
Are you cheating me from now?  <br><br>
